msg:Generally, I prefer to choose Hilton when traveling. This is my first time staying in the Huiting series. The environment and facilities are good, and the service staff are very polite. The service staff of Hilton hotels are all very polite.
1. This time I stayed in Hilton Huiting in Guiyang. The overall feeling was good. In particular, the ventilation and air permeability of the room was not very good. I felt stuffy and hot after taking a shower. The air conditioner was set to cooling or ventilation. It was hot air. Later, I had to open the window and stand by the window to breathe to recover. Since the window can only be pushed open a little and the air conditioner is turned off, the air circulation speed in the room is still relatively slow. Although there is an air purifier in the room, it is still difficult to solve the problem of stuffiness. I called the front desk twice that night for feedback. The front desk staff told me that Guiyang had cooled down in the past two days, so the heating was turned on. Later, the hotel turned on the air conditioner, and I could fall asleep. In summary, I think the air conditioner should have the function of heating and cooling, because after all, not every resident has a different body feeling. The air conditioner in the room should have the function of adjus**ent. Taking a step back, even if the air conditioner cannot be turned on, the stuffiness in the room should be improved in the future. Regarding this issue, the front desk staff also expressed sincere apologies when I checked out on the day of check-out, and gave me some small gifts. Ctrip customer service also called me several times to solve the problem for me and asked about my subsequent stay experience. I also compensated me. I like Ctrip's speed in solving the problem.
2. The breakfast is OK, with both Western and Chinese styles, and the variety is OK.
3. The Huiting series has a kitchen, a microwave, a small refrigerator, a coffee machine, and tableware. If it is a special recommendation for family travel, it is convenient for simple food heating. In addition to the standard mineral water, the bar also has two bottles of Evian every day. This is a thumbs upğŸ‘
4. The parking lot has ground and 4.5.6.7 floors to choose from. The parking spaces are still quite sufficient. It is recommended that the garage can be equipped with several always-on lighting. At present, the induction lighting is a bit short when returning to the hotel at night, which will be inconvenient.
5. The hotel should be located in a new development zone, so the surrounding facilities are still under construction.
Overall, it is still good. I hope Hilton Huiting can go to the next level.

When the front desk saw it, I asked if I would like a hot drink (this observation is also meticulous), and I felt warm in my heart. I also specifically asked about the names of these two service staff: Liu Lei, Zhou Xiaoli! Thumbs up for you. Later, I carelessly left my umbrella in the restaurant, and I thought I was in the car all the time. I didn't realize it until I got to the next station and was reminded by the Hilton staff!

It can be seen from the words in the pictures that the staff's intentions can be fully reflected. They pay attention to and observe every detail of the guests, and put them at ease. It is really worthy of praiseğŸ‘

Hygiene: Don't worry about hygiene, it's absolutely clean, don't worry.

Environment: First of all, the environment is absolutely fine, but there is one thing I want to mention, because I almost always choose Hilton hotels when I travel. This time, there is no special fragrance in the lobby (no smell), and the Hiltons I stayed in before are different. Types of aromatherapy scents.
